Wan Xuancai's Conversation Upon Arrival in Xuzhou 51

Detailed Account of Being Captured in Ningling

Yang Hongwei Also Escorted to Xuzhou at the Same Time

Xuzhou Correspondence – After Wan Xuancai was detained by Liu Maoen, Liu sent Adjutant Shi Dehai from Suixian to Liuhe the day before yesterday. There was Yang Hongwei, a counselor from Sun Chu's department, who was captured by the Third Division in Guide and held at the Second Army Corps headquarters. Liu Zhi then sent a special service battalion deputy, Wei Zhipeng, to escort Wan and Yang. The two arrived in Xuzhou by car at 8:00 PM last night (25th) and were immediately escorted to the Second Army Corps headquarters garrison office. Garrison Director Shen Maosheng telegraphed Liu Zhi for instructions and sent Wan and Yang to the army prison, placing them in the guard room with shackles on their feet. Wan is very tall and burly, 38 years old, a native of Song County. He was wearing a blue cloth student uniform top, gray Western-style twill military pants, black thread socks, and black straight-grained呢 short boots with buckles. During the conversation, he was straightforward and somewhat unrefined, but his demeanor was natural. According to Wan, (When I was chairman in Henan, I really didn't have much power. All the provincial tax collection agencies were taken over by Lu Zhonglin's people. Later, Lu sent people to Kaifeng to set up a military surcharge, which was too much, so I prohibited its establishment. The provincial government also failed to organize from beginning to end, being nominal but without substance, so there was no need to organize it. At the end of last month, my father passed away due to illness. I asked Yan for leave, but he didn't approve it, so I telegraphed Yan and returned to my hometown to arrange the funeral. After burying my father, my mother also became ill and passed away, and a son also died. Because my work was not going smoothly and my family was experiencing multiple misfortunes, I was very discouraged. My father's funeral was held on the 12th of this month. I only returned east on the 15th. On the 17th, I arrived at Liuhe. The forward units had already been defeated, and news was not being communicated. On the 19th, I took a car with three followers to Ningling to meet with Commander Liu Maoen. I discussed military affairs and my resignation with Liu. About two or three miles after leaving, Liu ordered a division commander to chase after me and invite me back, and I was immediately detained. I sent someone to discuss with Liu the possibility of joining in surrendering to the central government, but Liu never met with me and sent someone to escort me to the Second Army Corps headquarters and then to Xuzhou. As for the fighting in Henan this time, the forward units had no possibility of fighting. When I was in Bian, I repeatedly received orders to set out, but because there were no provisions, I couldn't go. Each unit was scolding each other by telegram every day, so there was no intention to fight. My troops were under the command of Yan, and Feng was very wary of my troops because my troops had captured many weapons from Feng's troops in western Henan and southern Shaanxi last year. I remember that when I was in Luoyang, I sent the director of political training to Tongguan to meet Feng. Feng said to him, "Tell Wan that there are still Northwest Army people. It's okay to let him defend Luoyang, and if he doesn't let him defend Luoyang, I will remove the obstacles." After this, my troops also stopped contacting Feng. If the military defense arrangement this time has Feng's troops focusing on the Pinghan Railway and Jin's troops focusing on the Longhai Railway, then there are heavy defenses built by Luo Wang on the Longhai Railway, relying on the Yellow River for defense. If Luo Wang attacks Bian, it shouldn't be a problem. When I was coming east, the Jin troops in front, nominally five armies, were actually only the strength of five divisions, mostly changing divisions into armies, changing names. Sun Liangcheng's troops were in the rear, reinforcing and focusing on the south of the railway line, with Weishi and Chenliu as the areas where Sun's troops were concentrated. If the Jin troops are assembled at Lanfeng and Luo Wang, the Jin troops' combat has three weaknesses: First, there is a shortage of grain and forage, requisitioning it locally, disturbing the people, and still feeling the shortage; second, the railway lines are long, the response is not swift, and the command is not unified; third, with the historical relationship between Yan and Feng, I'm afraid they may not be able to cooperate to the end. I haven't met Yan and Feng for a long time, so I don't dare to make conjectures, but it can be predicted.) I heard that Wan is now preparing to submit a report to Chiang, willing to serve the central government by attacking the enemy in the former units in Henan to atone for his previous mistakes. Yang Hongwei, a counselor of Sun Chu, lives in the medical room, wearing a gray military uniform, also with a physique like Wan's and a sharper tongue. According to him, (He is from Dezhou, Shandong, a graduate of the sixth class of the Baoding Military Academy. After the Northern Expedition, he taught at the Wuchang Military Officer Branch School and then went to various armies and divisions in Anhui and Henan provinces as a staff member. In the campaign to attack Feng last year, because he had old ties with Sun Chu, he was appointed as a counselor. This March, he followed Sun from Shunde to Zhengzhou. When the war broke out, he followed Sun to Bian. When ordered to go to Guide to see Wan Diunzon, Guide could no longer be defended, so he returned west on a small car via a roundabout route. He was captured by the Third Division engineers midway and escorted to the Army Corps headquarters and then to Xuzhou.) Yang is quite skilled in literature and wrote books on rough-edged paper while en route to entertain himself. His writing is still clear and has a scholarly air. (26th)

The Captured Wan Xuancai

Reasons for Increasing International Postage Rates 52

The Ministry of Transportation's Document to the Executive Yuan

The international postage rates for letters and parcels will be increased by one-third starting July 1st, which has been submitted by the Ministry of Transportation to the Executive Yuan for approval and promulgation. The original document from the Ministry of Transportation is as follows: (According to the Postal Administration, the international postage rates listed in the Sixth Class, Various Countries section of the postage rate list promulgated in Circular No. 70 originally stipulated that the postage for letters should be 25 centimes, equivalent to one dime in national currency, for each unit of weight of 20 grams. Other postage rates were specified according to the type of item. However, in recent years, the price of silver has gradually decreased, and the previous conversion rate has become noticeably different. Recently, the price of gold has risen repeatedly, and the silver exchange rate has fallen sharply. Every pound sterling is now worth fourteen or fifteen dollars in national currency, which means that every dollar is only equivalent to 0.724 French francs. Compared to the previous conversion rate of 2.50 French francs, the difference is considerable. Our country still collects international postage according to the original stipulated rates, resulting in a loss of 45%. Because the transportation fees that our country pays to the various member countries of the Universal Postal Union are all calculated according to the gold franc stipulated in the convention, the balance of income and expenditure has been reduced by 45%. The losses on international parcel postage are even greater. For example, the transportation fee to France for a parcel weighing less than one kilogram is 1.80 French francs. Based on the current calculation of one dollar equaling 0.724 French francs, it is necessary to pay 1.04 dollars, while the postage collected is only 0.72 dollars according to the original conversion rate, resulting in a difference of 0.32 dollars. The losses on parcels weighing less than five or ten kilograms and parcels sent to other countries are also considerable. In order to avoid continuing losses and to prevent further declines in the price of silver and to facilitate calculation, it is proposed to change the original conversion rate of one dollar equaling 2.50 French francs or ten dollars equaling one pound sterling to 1.50 dollars equaling 2.50 French francs or fifteen dollars equaling one pound sterling, in accordance with Article 30 of the International Postal Convention, to provide relief. If calculated according to this revised rate, one dollar in national currency is equal to 1.6666 French francs, which means that every French franc is equal to 0.60 dollars in national currency, and the postage for international letters with a weight of 20 grams should be changed from one dime to one and a half dimes. This revision of the conversion rate will also increase the collected international postage by 50%, and all international parcels will also be increased by 50%. Furthermore, after checking, the fee of one and a half dimes for international letters with a weight of 20 grams, equivalent to 25.86 centimes, is almost the same as the fee of 25 centimes charged by Japan, the United States, and Germany for each letter with a weight of 20 grams, and is even lower than that of countries such as England and France, so there is no conflict. In addition to the registration fee and express fee being increased last year and the parcels sent to the United States being handled according to the agreement without paying transportation fees to that country, the increase should be postponed. Furthermore, the postage rates for Japan, etc., in the Seventh Class and Hong Kong, etc., in the Eighth Class are specially stipulated and should be changed with the domestic rates and not be counted. Therefore, the reasons and related documents have been presented for your review and instructions.) Based on this, the Ministry has conducted a review and found that Article 29 of the Stockholm International Postal Convention states that the franc is recognized as the monetary standard in this Convention and various agreements, referring to the gold franc of one hundred centimes. Article 30 states that each member country of the Universal Postal Union should stipulate the postage rates in its current currency according to the most equal number of French francs in value. The original standard of our country's currency was the silver dollar. Before joining the Universal Postal Union, the conversion rate of the silver dollar was one silver dollar equal to 2.50 French francs (one French franc is one hundred centimes), or ten silver dollars equal to 25 French francs, which is also equal to one pound sterling. At that time, the postage rates for various international postal items were calculated according to this conversion rate, which is the most equal number of gold francs in value. Now, the price of gold has risen and the silver exchange rate has fallen, so it is necessary to revise the conversion rate in accordance with the International Postal Convention to make up for the losses. Furthermore, the commercial activities of foreigners in our country are becoming increasingly prosperous. After this revision, foreigners will bear about 95% of the increased fees, while the Chinese people will only bear about 5%. Therefore, this revision will not have any impact on the general public. The situation presented should be approved, and the attached table should be copied and presented to your esteemed Yuan for review and filing, and for instructions to be followed.

Explanation of the Assembly's Interpretation of the Trade Union Law (Continued) 53

(13) Regarding point thirteen, whether the trade union is absolutely prohibited from interfering with or obstructing the business of a member who has withdrawn from the union or been expelled, according to Article 20, the investigation of the Trade Union Law stipulates that trade unions must not interfere with or obstruct the work of workers, whether they have not joined the union or have joined and withdrawn, and this should be handled accordingly. (14) Regarding point fourteen, concerning remedial measures if the number of union members falls below the legal minimum due to employers inducing members to withdraw from the union, as stipulated in Article 21, the Trade Union Law stipulates that employers may not make withdrawal from the union a condition of employment. This restricts employer actions, and according to Article 1 of the Trade Union Law, the situation of the number of members falling below the legal minimum is unlikely to occur in reality. (15) Regarding point fifteen, that although a trade union member who has withdrawn from the union and continues to be an industrial or professional worker is not entitled to the protection of Section 4 of this law, should they be allowed to continue enjoying the general rights of workers obtained in mediation or arbitration under the name of the union in labor disputes before withdrawing, the investigation reveals that only Article 33 in Section 4 of the Trade Union Law concerns the protection of workers. Article 33 states that workers shall not be dismissed during the mediation or arbitration of labor disputes, and does not differentiate between union and non-union members; therefore, they should be treated equally, and those who have obtained the general rights of workers in mediation or arbitration should be allowed to continue enjoying them. (16) Regarding point sixteen, as stipulated in Article 38, trade unions may declare dissolution due to merger or separation, but Article 6 stipulates that only one trade union may be established for workers of the same profession or industry within the same region. It is therefore inappropriate to allow trade unions in the same industry to separate, or trade unions in different industries to merge. What does "merger" and "separation" refer to? The interpretation of merger and separation should be based on the provisions of Article 23 of the Implementing Regulations of the Trade Union Law. (17) Regarding point seventeen, if the competent authority deems it necessary for an established trade union to merge or separate, and the members of the relevant trade unions cannot agree, can it be enforced? The competent authority should have the power to enforce its decisions when it deems them necessary for the trade unions under its jurisdiction. (18) Regarding point eighteen, according to Article 6, only one trade union may be established for workers of the same profession or industry within the same region. Are there boundaries for what is meant by "same region"? According to Article 4, it seems that the province, city, and county are considered regions. A province contains multiple counties and ordinary cities and cannot be the unit of a trade union region. A city (special municipality and ordinary city) and a county may be interpreted as the same region. However, strictly speaking, it would be difficult in reality to have only one trade union for one industry within the city or county region. In mainland counties, regardless of how many villages and towns are included, even in the Shanghai Special Municipality, if the entire city is considered the same region, workers in each industry (industrial or professional) throughout the city can only form one trade union. For example, although there are city-wide cotton mill unions, city-wide silk mill unions, and city-wide cotton weaving mill unions, workers in each factory cannot establish individual unions, and the city cannot be divided into districts to establish district unions. Supervision would be difficult, and the organizational procedure of trade unions would lack a foundation. If there are already individual unions in various factories, should they all be dissolved and merged? What problems would arise from this implementation? The investigation reveals that the boundaries of this region should be determined by the competent authority in accordance with the provisions of Article 7 of the Implementing Regulations of the Trade Union Law, taking into account local circumstances and investigating customs and actual conditions. (19) Regarding point nineteen, according to Article 50, if a trade union council is punished, and there is more than one council member, should the punishment be carried out separately? If there is a violation of paragraph 1 of the same article, and there is no report or a false report regarding the matters in Article 51, and the penalty is enforced, but the trade union does not have the title of "council member" and its current staff only includes executive committee members and standing committee members, who should the aforementioned penalty apply to? When punishing trade union council members, the responsible council member should be punished separately. If there is no title of "council member," whoever performs the duties of a council member, regardless of the title, should be punished. (20) Regarding point twenty, if a trade union staff member or member violates the provisions of Articles 10, 13, 17, 18, 20, 22, and 23, and there are no penalty provisions, how should it be handled? If a trade union staff member or member violates the listed articles, the competent authority should handle it according to the severity of the circumstances, issuing a prohibition for minor violations or dissolving the union in accordance with Article 37 of the Trade Union Law for serious violations. Violations of Article 13 are not effective, and members can supervise violations of Article 18 themselves. (21) Regarding point twenty-one, trade unions established before the implementation of this law must have already had elected staff. If they are required to re-register according to the procedures of Article 5 within two months in accordance with the provisions of Article 51, should they be required to revert to the initial stage of launching and re-elect representatives to apply for registration, or should the original staff be responsible for applying for registration according to the procedures? The original staff should be responsible for applying for registration according to the procedures. The above is an explanation of the various points of doubt regarding the Trade Union Law presented by the Shanghai Special Municipality Government and forwarded by the Executive Yuan. Furthermore, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce submitted a petition to the Executive Yuan stating that the issue of trade union regions is not only whether they should be divided within a city or county. It is necessary to clearly explain how to determine the region when the scope of an industry exceeds one county or one city, or one province or one special municipality, and which authority should approve it. Furthermore, Article 4 of the Trade Union Law stipulates that the competent supervisory authority of a trade union is the provincial, municipal, or county government where it is located. However, if the scope of an industry exceeds one province or one special municipality, which authority should be in charge of supervision? Furthermore, Article 51 of the Trade Union Law stipulates that trade unions established before the implementation of this law should re-register from the date of implementation, otherwise they will be subject to the penalties of Article 50 of the same law. However, since the implementation of the Trade Union Law, cases involving interpretations of doubts in various provinces and cities have been difficult to resolve in a timely manner, often exceeding the time limit stipulated in Article 51. Can an extension be granted? These three items are difficult for the Ministry to independently draft reasonable solutions, so they are submitted together with the list opened by the Shanghai Special Municipality Government regarding points 18, 19, 20, and 21 for special consultation with the Legislative Yuan for review. The investigation reveals that the competent authority should determine how to delineate the trade union region in accordance with the provisions of Article 7 of the Implementing Regulations of the Trade Union Law, taking into account the circumstances. As for whether an extension can be granted because cases involving interpretations of doubts in various provinces and cities have been difficult to resolve in a timely manner since the implementation of the Trade Union Law, often exceeding the time limit stipulated in Article 51, an application should be submitted to the National Government for consideration in accordance with the provisions of Article 24 of the Implementing Regulations of the Trade Union Law.

Anniversary of the Shandong Provincial Government's Move to Jinan 54

Jinan Correspondence: Since the May Third Incident, Jinan was occupied by Japanese soldiers, and the Shandong Provincial Government was temporarily established in Tai'an. All facilities were makeshift. The provincial government did not begin to move from Tai'an to Jinan on May 25 until last year, when Jinan was recovered and the Japanese soldiers withdrew. Time has passed quickly, and the first anniversary has arrived in an instant. The provincial government specially held a commemorative meeting in the main auditorium of the government office at 9:00 a.m. today (the 26th). A colorful archway was erected at the entrance of the provincial government office, inscribed with the words "Anniversary of the Shandong Provincial Government's Move to Jinan." Party and national flags were hung crisscrossed. The government office was decorated with lanterns and colors, which was extremely lively. More than a thousand people from various agencies attended. Chairman Zhu Xi opened the meeting and saluted, followed by a memorial week. He Siyuan reported on party affairs, and Zhu Xi reported on politics and military affairs. Then, a commemorative ceremony was held for the provincial government's move to Jinan. Zhu Xi reported on the significance of the commemoration, stating briefly that today's commemorative meeting is to commemorate the Shandong Provincial Government's move from Tai'an to Jinan on this day last year. Looking back on the work of the past year, whether it can satisfy the hopes of the people, all construction has not reached the original plan, which is really regrettable. However, in this year, on the one hand, taxes have been reorganized, and on the other hand, construction has been actively undertaken. Special attention has been paid to the previous suffering of the people, and efforts have been made to reduce the burden on the people. This is a regret that can still be reassuring. The comrades of the provincial government are appointed by the central government, and they should strive to carry out their responsibilities. In the future, there will be comprehensive plans for civil administration, construction, education, agriculture, mining, and commerce, which will be announced soon. Next, representatives of the Provincial Rectification Committee, He Siyuan, and members of the Provincial Government, Chen Mingyu, spoke in succession. The meeting adjourned with slogans at 11:00 a.m. After the adjournment, the provincial government also performed various recreational activities and dramas and opened for sightseeing for one day. All agencies were closed today, and shops also hung flags to celebrate (May 26th).

Passage of Vietnamese Aircraft Team Through Guangdong 55

Guangzhou Correspondence: The Vietnamese government of French Indochina has an established aviation team. Recently, the aircraft team, considering the close relationship between Guangdong Province and Vietnam in terms of business and economy, launched a tour of Guangdong. Three French aviators, divided into two-seater Breuleux biplanes, came to Guangdong. The Vietnamese government first consulted with our Ministry of Foreign Affairs to notify the Central Aviation Administration and then instructed the Guangdong Aviation Office to inform them. After receiving the telegram, the Aviation Office dispatched several Guangdong aircraft teams to meet them in the air and guide the French aircraft. As expected, at 8:00 a.m. on the 21st, the group of three aircraft departed from Annam and flew towards Guangzhou. At 2:30 p.m., two aircraft safely landed at the Dashatou Airfield. In addition, one aircraft went missing in the Guangzhou Prefecture. Upon landing in Guangzhou, the two Vietnamese aircraft were received by the head of the Guangdong Aviation Office, the captain of the aircraft team, and others, and visited the Guangdong aviation agencies and repair shops. The French aviators were disheartened by the loss of one aircraft and hastily went to the French Consulate in Shamian to rest and report the circumstances of the missing aircraft. The French Consul formally notified the Guangdong administrative agencies to order a joint investigation. On the afternoon of the 22nd, the French Consul received a telegram from Macau stating that the missing Vietnamese aircraft had landed 80 kilometers from Macau. The aircraft was slightly damaged, but the two Frenchmen driving the aircraft were fortunately unharmed. They walked to Macau on the same day and took a boat to Guangzhou on the 24th. (It is reported that the Vietnamese aircraft fell from the sky at 3:00 p.m. on the 21st in Datouwan in Nanlang Township, Zhongshan County. Fortunately, the landing site was a paddy field with tall rice stalks, and the geology was cement, so the aircraft was only slightly damaged when it fell. Both French aviators were in the aircraft, one with a nose injury and the other safe and sound. The villagers who saw the crash reported it to the local police, who dispatched a team to protect the site and report it to the county government. The two French aviators believed that the site was not far from Macau and transportation was convenient, so they volunteered to take a boat from Macau to Guangzhou to meet with the aviator who had come with them before returning to Vietnam together.) After arriving in the province, the two men met their companions and celebrated with relief. Today (24th), they jointly performed aviation stunts in Guangzhou with the aviators and explained the contents of the Vietnamese aircraft to the aviation personnel here. In the evening, Chairman Chen of the Provincial Government hosted a banquet to welcome the French aviators and invited personnel from the Aviation Office to attend in order to strengthen diplomatic relations. It is reported that the Vietnamese aircraft are scheduled to fly back to Vietnam via Guangzhou Bay tomorrow (25th) (May 24th).

The Process of Financial Reorganization in Heilongjiang Province 56

Related to the Safety and Stability of the Economy of Northern Manchuria

The Current and Past Finances of Heilongjiang Province

Heilongjiang Correspondence: In recent months, the value of banknotes issued in Heilongjiang has been declining, causing significant losses to farmers. Pang Zuoping, member of the Heilongjiang Provincial Government and Director of the Finance Department, believed that this matter was related to the local economy. If no measures were taken to maintain it, the harm to the people in the future would be unimaginable. Therefore, he proposed a relief plan at the 73rd meeting of the provincial government, which was passed. Because this case is related to the safety and stability of the economy of Northern Manchuria, the proposal and the report of the Director of the Finance Department are recorded below: Proposal 1: It is proposed that the price of silver is increasing daily and the price of money is falling, causing difficulties for officials and civilians. If we want to find a fundamental solution, there is no better way than thoroughly reorganizing the finances. The method of reorganizing the finances has been submitted to the financial conference, and the reasons why we dare not raise the legal price and the situation of deficits in the treasury have been submitted separately for discussion in order to seek relief. However, the recent surge in the price of silver is even worse, with each yuan rising by twenty or thirty strings in a single day. The people's hearts are shaken and there is a great momentum that cannot be stopped. Detailed observation of the situation in this province is not comparable to other places. Since there is no place for currency transactions, there are few merchants who are trying to profit. Although there are a few who buy and sell Jiang money, it should not be so suspicious that money tickets will continue to be issued. The Guangxin Company has a printing press dedicated to printing money tickets. The general merchants and people are suspicious of this, thinking that the machine-made money tickets are being produced in large quantities every day, and it is natural that the value will continue to decline. The crowd is panicked and wary. This kind of rumor is easy to breed bewilderment, so public sentiment is declining day by day, and the price of silver must be soaring. (2) Unclear about the truth of the finances. The province's finances have been in deficit for a long time. Whenever there are large amounts of money needed, the Guangxin Company has to borrow. This cannot be concealed. However, in the past two years, the finances have been reorganized and there has been a turnaround. The income and expenditure are offset, and there is a surplus. Not only are the daily military and political expenses paid at any time, but also the various expenses during last year's Russian riot were reluctantly dealt with, and no points were borrowed from the company. Outsiders cannot know the truth in this regard. They all say that the government's deficit is borrowed from the Guangxin Company, and that last year's defense of Russia used a lot of money. Where does the company's money come from? It is nothing more than issuing money tickets to meet the urgent need. This kind of argument is all unclear about the truth. How can we blame them? Although the above two reasons are not the root cause of the financial riots, they also have a great impact. Without faith, the country cannot stand. Finances should be made public. If we do not break this doubt and declare the truth, how can we show great faith and dispel the doubts of the people? It is proposed that the provincial government order the supervisor and the Guangxin Company to regularly convene the banking community and the commercial and agricultural associations to close the Guangxin Company's ticket printing machine to show their determination not to continue issuing money tickets, and to announce the financial situation of the past two years on the spot so that the merchants and people can know the truth and no longer suspect, which may be able to maintain the hearts of the people and save them from one or two. Is it appropriate to submit it to the conference for public resolution?

Proposal 2: It is proposed that the province's currency system has always been based on Jiang money. In the 10th year of the Republic of China, in order to provide relief to the finances, the Guangxin Company was approved to issue current silver dollar coupons to circulate alongside Jiang money. However, the amount of silver dollar notes issued was not large, and they could not be promoted throughout the province. The circulation in various counties and cities still relies on Jiang money. All county bureaus collect all taxes, except for Heilongjiang, Hulun, Anda, Yalu, Lubin, Hulun, Shiwei, Qigan, and Zhaodong, where the promotion of silver dollars does not cause problems. Although the revenue from other county bureaus has been changed to silver dollars, they actually collect Jiang money. Jiang money must be priced at a legal price as a basis for conversion to silver dollars. In the past, when the price of silver was stable, the legal price was slightly higher than the market price to avoid losses in the treasury. However, when the situation suddenly changed last winter, the price of silver gradually increased. At that time, the legal price was 290 strings, although it was lower than the market price, it showed that we dared not increase it lightly, fearing that it would shake the hearts of the people and make it more chaotic. When the situation was slightly calmer, the price of silver continued to rise. If the legal price is increased accordingly, the people's hearts will become more and more virtual, the price of money will fall more and more, and what will become of the financial future? I inspected the market situation and reported to the chairman that I would not increase the legal price in order to maintain the financial situation. After several months, the treasury suffered hidden losses, which was huge. This situation has been reported repeatedly. Now the price of silver has risen to more than 440 strings, exceeding the legal price by more than 150 strings, and the treasury loss has increased as a result. As of now, it is estimated that the loss has been about 2 million yuan. If the legal price was increased step by step at that time, there would be no such loss. How can we not? However, where will the people take the loss? It can be said that this sacrifice of the government is to cultivate the vitality of the people, or it can be said to reduce the burden on the people. However, this loss is tangible and easily detected. If the legal price was also increased at that time, the situation would be intertwined and continue until today. How high would the price of silver have risen? The burden on the merchants and people of the province would be extremely heavy, and the loss would be endless. The so-called people's power and commerce would not be exhausted and decline. The deeper the accumulated illness, the more difficult it is to reorganize. Not only is the gold broken and there is no way to clean up, but also the income from all taxes will inevitably be sharply reduced, and the treasury will be invisible

Page 10

The loss may be more than this number. The weight and the gains and losses are weighed. It is difficult to avoid losses in the treasury. Now, Wangkui, Zhaozhou, and other counties have requested to increase the legal price because the legal price is too low and it is difficult to maintain local police studies. The investigation shows that the situation is true in that county, and the same is true in other counties. Although we dare not immediately discuss the increase, we should carefully plan a good method. In the long run, it is not a good strategy. The fundamental solution lies in reorganizing the finances. All the methods for reorganizing the finances have been submitted to the financial conference. I will not repeat them here. However, the financial problem needs time to be resolved. What should be done to remedy the current situation in order to achieve comprehensive planning? The matter is of great importance and should be submitted to the conference for discussion. Please make a public decision. (To be continued)

Anhui's Meeting on Cutting Li Tax and Special Tax 57

Wuhu Correspondence: The Ministry of Finance has decided to implement the national cut of the Li tax and the addition of special taxes on October 10, and has ordered the commissioner's offices of finance in each province to organize special consumption tax committees to prepare everything. The Anhui commissioner's office organized the committee on the 22nd and followed the rules of the ministry to divide into four sections: general affairs, investigation, review, and compilation. The general affairs section is in charge of documents and other matters. The investigation section is in charge of the current value of various goods and local sales, local production for export, local production for export to foreign countries, foreign provinces for import, foreign provinces for transit, the types and quantities of goods imported from overseas, and the opinions of merchants and people in the province on the cutting of the Li tax. The review section is in charge of the taxation tax rate, the location of the bureaus, etc. The compilation section is in charge of statistical forecasting tables. In addition to the commissioners' offices designating a number of people, the Wuhu General Chamber of Commerce and the Anhui Provincial Chamber of Commerce also nominated Yuan Doushu, Tao Yutang, She Ceqin, Li Dachu, Li Yuwen, and others to join. The first committee meeting was held at 2:00 p.m. today (26th). More than 20 people attended. Bao Geng, the second section chief of the special office, chaired the meeting. After discussion, it was agreed that the revenue from the Li tax in Anhui Province, including the seven items of unified tax on sugar, tea, hemp, minerals, silk, cocoons, fragrant wood, and eggs (annual levy of 600,000 yuan), totals 3.16 million yuan per year. If the Li tax is cut, the tax revenue from the 19 special consumption taxes (sugar, textiles, wool products, oil, tea, paper, tin foil, seafood, timber, porcelain, livestock, medicine, lacquer, fur, large minerals, cocoons, silk, soybeans, and cotton) will only be about 600,000 yuan. Moreover, the commerce of Anhui Province is dominated by rice. Since rice is not taxed, the tax will inevitably be sharply reduced. However, the Ministry of Finance still needs to allocate 1.6 million yuan to Anhui Province after the cutting of the Li tax. This shortage of 1 million yuan has been ordered to prepare a business tax. The business tax is borne by the sedentary merchants. In this autumn of declining commerce, if the burden on the sedentary merchants is increased, the local area may be affected. The majority of the provinces advocate the implementation of the inland consumption tax to compensate for the 1 million yuan. Therefore, the investigation and review sections of the committee are both important. The Provincial Chamber of Commerce and the General Chamber of Commerce plan to nominate members to participate in the special committee. The rules stipulate that meetings are held once a day. Now, because the General Chamber of Commerce and the Provincial Chamber of Commerce must hold meetings tomorrow to discuss and nominate members of the two sections, the meeting will be suspended for one day tomorrow (28th).

Agreed Measures for the Second Phase of Price Stabilization: The director of the charity granary management committee, Shao Keran, convened district chiefs to discuss measures for the second phase of price stabilization: (1) Each person will receive four catties of rice at the same price as the first phase, 160 cash per catty. The start date will be determined as soon as possible. (2) Districts that have not yet collected the full amount of rice money from the first phase must do so by May 31st. (3) The 20,000 yuan loss from the two price stabilization efforts this year will be submitted to the county for inclusion in the 19th-year local budget to be compensated. (4) Households that did not purchase rice in the first phase may combine their purchases in the second phase; those that still do not purchase rice by the second phase will be given a deadline by the district office and considered to have voluntarily given up their right to purchase. Additional Notes on Robbery Cases in Various Townships: Robbery cases have been occurring frequently in the east and west townships recently. For example, in Sanguantang, the homes of Ruan Zhihuai and Qian Chuntang were robbed in one night. The homes of Xia Tu in Cao Shi Tu Thirty-nine Tu, Chen Heshang Fang Sixteen Tu, and Han Erxiang were also robbed one after another, with estimated losses of three to four hundred yuan each.

Jiading 62

Telephone Connection Between Jiading and Xiang: The County Construction Bureau is making great efforts to install public telephones. The Jia'an line was connected to Waigang on the 15th. The Jiading-Xiang telephone line has now been installed and was connected the day before yesterday. It is also reported that the Nanxiang-Ji Wang line may be connected today (the 29th).

Taking Over the Nanxiang Sports Field: The Nanxiang Public Sports Field was transferred to the county administration by the County Education Bureau upon the request of the district office. Director Yang forwarded the request to the Education Department for approval and has received instructions to proceed accordingly. The Education Bureau has appointed Qian Wenrui as the director of the field. On the 28th, the director of the Public Education Center, Lu Linxun, together with the director, went to take over the field.

Wuxi 63

Execution of the Notorious Communist Cai Yingzhang: Cai Yingzhang, a notorious Communist in this county, colluded with the executed bandits Zhu Dingbao, Qian Zhiyi, Yan Ating, and others two years ago to carry out large-scale riots in Chensifang, Zhajiaqiao, Anzhen, and other places in the northeast township, killing, setting fires, and looting property. The provincial government offered a reward for his capture. Last year, Wu Zhengrong, the chief of the county government's political police, led police officers Cao Zhonglie and Wen Ziming to arrest Cai Yingzhang in the British concession in Shanghai's Dongxinqiao. Cai was escorted back to Wuxi and interrogated by the county government. Cai confessed to the riots. Recently, County Magistrate Sun, considering Cai's crimes to be heinous and inexcusable, recorded his confession and telegraphed the provincial government for review. The provincial government replied with a death sentence. After receiving the telegram from the provincial government, County Magistrate Sun dispatched police to tie up Cai Yingzhang and execute him by firing squad at the South School Field yesterday (the 28th) at 10 a.m. to serve as a warning.

Scheduled Opening of Wuxi-Cheng Long-Distance Bus Service: The southern section of the Wuxi-Cheng Highway within this county is nearing completion since construction began. The northern section within Jiangyin County is expected to be completed within the year. Last autumn, Feng Xiaozhong and Fei Shenchu from Shanghai, along with Sun Chenchu from this county, initiated the organization of the Wuxi-Cheng Long-Distance Bus Company to operate passenger and freight services. They planned to raise 100,000 yuan by issuing 2,000 shares, initially collecting half the price. They also obtained approval from the Construction Department for exclusive operating rights for three years. The company first established a preparatory office in Shanghai to actively raise funds. On the 20th of this month, the preparatory office was moved to Wuxi and a site was rented next to the railway police station on Chezhan Road to construct the Wuxi-Cheng Long-Distance Bus Terminal. Construction is scheduled to begin within a week and be completed in two months. Hua Zhengxia and Yu Heqin, resident representatives in Wuxi, are responsible for supervision. Eight long-distance buses have been ordered from a foreign firm in Shanghai and are scheduled to arrive in July. Passenger service will begin between Wuxi and Yanqiao in this county. Once the northern section is completed, service will extend directly to Jiangyin.

Investigation of Residents from North of the Yangtze River: The County Public Security Bureau, noting the influx of residents from north of the Yangtze River to Wuxi in recent years, with a mixture of good and bad, and the current unrest due to bandits, has ordered its various branches to conduct a thorough investigation and registration. The urban area has now been surveyed. The first branch in the urban area has jurisdiction over more than 800 households, the second branch in the Malu area has more than 400 households, the third branch in the southern area has more than 1,200 households, the fourth branch in the western area has more than 1,400 households, the fifth branch in the northern area has more than 500 households, the sixth branch in the Guangqin area has more than 1,000 households, the first directly-administered branch has more than 650 households, the ninth branch has more than 300 households, and the tenth branch has more than 100 households. The urban area has a total of more than 6,500 households. The rural area is currently being actively surveyed and registered, with the northern townships reportedly having the most residents.

Appeal in Case of Impersonating an Official to Defraud Money: Jiang Rongxian from Jiangwan colluded with his wife, Gu Xiuyu, falsely claiming to be related to former Civil Affairs Director Bin, to help Yang Gubai from Liyang secure the position of chief of the Nanhui Public Security Bureau, defrauding him of 1,000 yuan. After the case was exposed, the county sentenced Jiang Jingxian to one year of imprisonment and a fine of 500 yuan, and ordered him to repay Yang Gubai 1,000 yuan. Jiang declared his dissatisfaction in court and filed an appeal within the prescribed time. The Wuxian District Court summoned witnesses the day before yesterday to open a trial for questioning. The court ordered Jiang Jingxian to find a reliable guarantor for temporary release pending judgment.

Changzhou 64

Raid on Kidnapping Ring Outside the North Gate: A kidnapping gang recently infiltrated the Shizhuzitou nunnery on Lower Street outside the North Gate of Wu County and secretly set up a base. The kidnappers, led by Liu Shaoyun from Henan, colluded with local ruffians like Chao Cunkun to act as guides. On the 26th, they hired a boat to kidnap the female nun Kuang Haiyi and her disciple Zhi De from the Xijuzi Bureau behind Baizhang Town, and also kidnapped the wife of farmer Liu Jinsheng from Tanjia Village. They robbed all their belongings, tied them up, and loaded them onto the boat, heading towards the city and hiding in the Shizhuzitou nunnery. At 11 a.m. on the 27th, Jin Dejin, the patrol chief of the third stationed post of the first public security bureau, secretly reported this after discovering it. Patrol Officer Wang Minwei immediately led police to search the premises and apprehended the kidnapper Chao Xingkun, the female kidnapper Chao Sunshi, and the shelter provider, the nun Dao Liang, on the spot. They rescued the female kidnap victims Kuang Haiyi, her disciple Zhi De, and the Liu Chen family of three. It was then discovered that a boat used by the kidnappers was docked at the Jiangyin Wharf. Patrol Officer Wang ordered employee Yao Bojun to lead police to intercept the boat and apprehended the suspected criminals Sun Jingui and Xu Zhoushi on the boat, and they were taken to the bureau for custody. Patrol Officer Wang, together with Yao Shunchen, the head of Qingshan Town, and the town guards, then went to the nunnery and found stolen goods, military uniforms, and a wooden fake seal of the Third Regiment of the Jiangsu Provincial Security Force, as well as a small wooden fake official seal of Zhao Feipeng, and brought them back to the bureau. At about 6 p.m., after preliminary trials of the kidnappers and kidnap victims separately, a document was prepared and sent to the Public Security Bureau for further investigation.

Jiangyin 65

Joint Defense of Cheng, Jing, and Tai Counties: Due to the rampant banditry in Jing and Tai counties north of the Yangtze River, County Magistrate Wang of Jingjiang initiated a joint defense plan for the three counties of Cheng, Jing, and Tai. County Magistrate Li expressed his approval and decided to assist to the best of his ability within the realm of possibility. Unclear Cause of Death of a Sand Laborer: On the 20th, the De Shun Township Hucao Port Security Corps detained a suspect named Shi Daguan. His family requested bail through the district chief, requiring a fee of eight yuan, which caused delays. While detained by the corps, the corps leader Chen Songshan allegedly used torture during interrogation. Yesterday (the 27th) morning, Shi's body was found hanging from a tree half a li from the corps headquarters, with injuries all over. His family reported this to the district chief, who forwarded it to the county. A coroner will be sent to the village today to investigate.

Nantong 66

Bandits Captured and Executed in Qian’an: The military and police have been victorious in suppressing bandits in the eastern townships for several days, capturing many. In the Qian’an district, they intercepted the bandit leaders Ge Hongfei and Zhang Bohe, who confessed without hesitation and were executed on the spot.

Donations Solicited to Expand the County Police Force: With rampant banditry throughout the county, representatives from all sectors agreed to expand the county police force. The required funds for weapons, ammunition, and uniforms, totaling 40,000 yuan, will be divided among wealthy individuals for donation, to be collected within five days for immediate use.

Reassignment of Branch Directors in the County Public Security Bureau: The County Public Security Bureau reassigned the directors of the fifth district public security branches on the 27th: Yu Dongjiang, Zhushigang; Zhang Shushen, Jinsha; Zhu Tingshi, Lujinggang; Zhang Songting, Xiting; Fan Kang.

Assignment of District Party Committee Members Throughout the County: The positions of the County Reorganization Committee members throughout the county have been determined, and the duties have been assigned to the standing committee members of each district as follows: Wang Tao for District 1, Ma Zhu for District 2, Ni Guoxiang for Districts 3 and 4, and Chen Gongdu for District 7.

Case of Police Officers Killed in Action While Suppressing Bandits: County Police Captain Jin Juechen reported to the county government that several dozen police officers were killed in action while suppressing bandits in Sijiaba during the tenure of former Captain Yan, requesting compensation. However, local sources report that bandits seized over one hundred rifles and pistols from the police during the Sijiaba battle, and that the police offered no resistance. Furthermore, no bodies were found afterward. The county government has ordered Captain Jin to investigate whether the police officers deserted.

Rugao 67

County Representative Assembly: The third county representative assembly was held in this county on the afternoon of the 25th. More than 20 representatives attended. Dong Xiao, Su Cao, and Hong Ci were elected as the presidium. Xu Yanjun was assigned by the provincial party headquarters as the assembly instructor.

Bizarre Xu Cai Case: Huang Jikang and other local ruffians, impersonating public security bureau officials, colluded with Gu and others to swindle the monk Rongzhai of Wenfeng Pavilion without success and were arrested for investigation.

Change of Trial Official: Li Weiyuan, the trial official of this county, resigned to the High Court and was approved. The vacancy will be filled by Sun Lüsan, former member of the Suqian case clearance committee.

Zhenjiang 68

Bandits Continuously Rob Security Corps in Gaozi Township: Last night (the 26th) around 12:00 AM, a large gang of more than a hundred bandits suddenly arrived in the Weigang area of the third district of Gaozi Township, Zhenjiang. They first went to the security corps and robbed four rifles, three pistols, and two handguns. They then went to the Tanggang security corps in the second district and robbed 19 rifles and 8 pistols, and abducted three corps members and one platoon leader. Afterward, they went to the Caijiazhuang security corps and robbed 10 rifles and 5 pistols. The three places that were robbed successively reported to the Zhenjiang County Government. Upon hearing the news, the county government immediately requested the Civil Affairs Department to dispatch a team to Zhenjiang.

Closing of County Representative Assembly: The third county representative assembly of Zhenjiang opened on the 25th. It is reported that yesterday morning, the representatives continued discussions until about 5:00 PM when the various proposals were discussed. Then, an election of executive and supervisory committee members was held. As a result, Chen Sibai, Liu Jian, Hu Jianmin, Dai Jingnian, and Wu Lianqing were elected as executive committee members. Yang Gongyai, Dong Guozhang, Zhuang Meifang, and others were elected as supervisory committee members. The closing ceremony was held at 11:00 AM.

Change of Zhenjiang Customs Commissioner: Moore, the Zhenjiang Customs Commissioner, has served in Zhenjiang for a long time. He has been ordered to be transferred to Beihai Customs. The vacancy will be filled by the Japanese Kitahama Sachiyuki, the Dalian Customs Commissioner, who will arrive in Zhenjiang soon.

Yangzhou 69

Slaughter Tax Receives No Bids: The county government, with the approval of the Provincial Education Management Office, ordered Gu Yunpeng to come to Yangzhou to meet with the county to re-invite merchants to bid on the slaughter tax after the original merchant, Yao Yiming, resigned. However, the tax amount was increased during the off-season, and the requirement to purchase 24 coupons was added on the 25th. Yesterday (the 26th), the county government telegraphed the Provincial Education Management Office to request instructions to reschedule the bidding or compel the original merchant to resume operation in order to ensure tax revenue.

Finance Bureau Meeting on Returning Acreage Tax: The Finance Bureau, in compliance with the county government's order, reported that former Director Jingzhong had misappropriated the acreage tax during his tenure. Now that Committee Member Shou of the Construction Department has demanded its return, it should be repaid by ordering the current Director Yu to convene a meeting of the local agencies that receive funds to designate local county funds for repayment. Therefore, a meeting of representatives from the local agencies receiving funds was convened at the bureau at 2:00 PM on the 27th, and a comparative table of local fees and expenditures during Fang's tenure was distributed on the spot for discussion. However, no concrete solutions were reached temporarily.

Huzhou 70

Zhaofeng Cocoon Firm Completely Burned Down: The Zhaofeng Cocoon Firm, located in Yangjiabu outside the West Gate of this city, is owned by the wealthy Wang family of this city and has sufficient capital. At about 4:00 AM this morning, a fire suddenly broke out in the firm's cocoon-drying room due to carelessness. Most of the firm's employees were awakened from their dreams. Due to the strong wind and the firm's location in a remote area, there was no way to extinguish the fire. It continued to burn until about 9:00 AM when it gradually died out. It is reported that the firm's buildings and the dry cocoons collected in recent days were all burned to the ground, resulting in a total loss of five or six thousand taels of silver. Fortunately, no one was injured, which is the only silver lining in this unfortunate event.

Hangzhou 71

Provincial Troops Enter Wenzhou to Suppress Bandits: The Zhejiang Provincial Government, due to the outbreak of banditry in Tao Shan area, Rui'an County, Wenzhou Prefecture, with over a thousand bandits seizing weapons from the Public Security Bureau and killing the Public Security Branch Chief Tan Huaisheng, aiming for a large-scale defense, urgently telegraphed Gan Qingchi, the commander of the Fourth Security Regiment, yesterday to lead his troops back to Wenzhou to suppress and defend, and report details within days.

Allocation of Water Conservancy Subsidies: The Zhejiang Western Water Conservancy Council submitted a request to the Construction Department yesterday to sign and issue over 90,000 yuan in water conservancy subsidies for sixteen cities and counties in western Zhejiang over the past two years, to be sent to banks for separate preservation.

Investigation of Public and Private Pawnshops: According to the latest survey by the Suggestions Department, there are pawnshops established in 41 counties in the province, including two public and thirty-three private.

Ningbo 72

Revoking the Ningbo Municipal Government: Regarding the case of the former application by the Executive Committee of Zhongyin County to the Provincial Executive Committee to the Provincial Government to revoke the Ningbo Municipal Government and merge it with the Yin County Government, the 109th Executive Committee meeting of the Provincial Executive Committee has passed the resolution and has forwarded a letter to the Provincial Government for consideration.

Major Personnel Changes on the Yongcao Road: The various branches of the Yongcao Railway Bureau have been ordered to reorganize and will be implemented at the beginning of next month. It is reported that the largest number of personnel changes will be in the Engineering Department, with little change in other departments.

Summary of Bandit Robberies: The home of Wen Zhou Asan, who lives in the Deng Feng Family Cemetery Village outside the North Gate of Cicheng, was suddenly attacked by several bandits the other night. They smeared Zhu Hei on their staffs, held torches, and broke into the house, intending to rob. Asan slipped out the door, beat a gong, and alerted the neighborhood. When the neighbors gathered with weapons, the bandits fled in alarm. One of the bandits, wearing a tattered military uniform, walked slower and was injured in the back of his hand and leg by the villagers. He was captured and sent to the county government yesterday morning for legal processing. Also, the Fumi Rice Shop in Jingcheng Head, Sanxikou, Southern Township of Yuyao, was suddenly attacked by five bandits posing as customers around 11:00 PM the other night. The shop owner, Zhao Erzhen, opened the door and was shocked to see robbers. The bandits rushed in and ransacked the counter, finding only a dozen or so silver dollars, which did not satisfy them. They then cut Erzhen with a knife and forced him to lead them to his house. Erzhen, forced by the violence of the thugs, had no choice but to lead the bandits to the home of Huang Zitan, allowing them to search and rob until 2:00 AM yesterday morning, when they left with a whoop. Upon inspection afterward, four rings, two pairs of gold bracelets, dozens of pieces of clothing, and more than 150 yuan in cash were stolen.

China & South Sea Bank to Establish a Ningbo Branch: The China & South Sea Bank headquarters in Shanghai believes that Ningbo is one of the trading ports where various banks have branches. Given the large amount of China & South Sea Bank banknotes circulating in Ningbo, it is necessary to establish a branch to facilitate cashing and remittances. It is reported that Yu Zuoting, the manager of Tianyi Zhuang, has been hired as the manager of the Ningbo branch. Mr. Yu is reportedly looking for a suitable location.

Xiaoshan 73

Dispute Over Converting Farmland into an Experimental Farm: After the Xiaoshan County Government reclaimed more than 50 mu of farmland outside the North Gate to convert it into an agricultural experimental farm, the local villagers strongly opposed it. Later, Wang Xiufu, the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, intervened and resolved the issue by having the county government purchase the permanent tenancy rights for 30 yuan per mu. However, the farmers were dissatisfied with the county government's payment of half in cash and half in promissory notes. On the one hand, they continued to petition the provincial government, claiming that reclaiming the original tenancy rights would cut off their livelihood, and requesting the provincial government to order the county to stop the conversion.

Businesses Change to Three-Term Account Collection: Since switching to the Gregorian calendar, Xiaoshan businesses have changed the collection of accounts at the Dragon Boat Festival, Mid-Autumn Festival, winter solstice, and year-end to three terms: the end of May, the end of September, and the end of December. The accounts of all businesses are scheduled to be collected at the end of May this time. In addition to distributing account statements to all customers, all outstanding accounts must be paid before June 1st.

The Second District Executive Committee Accuses the County Magistrate of Negligence: Shen Zhenfeng, a member of the Xiaoshan Eastern Township Party, accused County Magistrate Du of illegally arresting party members. He requested the Second District Executive Committee to promptly forward an accusation to the provincial party headquarters that County Magistrate Du Shihua was guilty of negligence and abuse of power by illegally detaining comrades working for the party.

Xinwan Township Requests Allocation of Affordable Rice: The Xinwan Township Farmers' Association, citing the poor land and poverty of the local people, requested the County Executive Committee to allocate 300 dan of affordable rice to the township to maintain the people's livelihood. The case has been forwarded by the committee to the Civil Food Committee for allocation. It is reported that a preliminary investigation of impoverished households will be conducted in accordance with procedures to ensure that no one is left out.

Xuzhou 74

Order to Relocate Zhang Xun's Memorial Hall: The Tongshan County Government, in compliance with the Civil Affairs Department's directive to permanently use Zhang Xun's memorial hall as the site for the Xuzhou Women's Middle School Experimental Elementary School, ordered the Red Swastika Society residing in the hall yesterday to relocate as soon as possible. However, today (the 26th), they received another directive from the Education Department, ordering the county magistrate to hand over Zhang Xun's memorial hall to the women's school within ten days of receiving the document and report back to the department.

Tokyo, This Newspaper, 28th: The Women's Volleyball Demonstration Tournament between China, Japan, and the Philippines adopts a double round-robin system. Therefore, after winning the match against China yesterday, it has been decided that Japan will win the Women's Volleyball Championship. Today's match between Japan and the Philippines will not affect the championship.

Tokyo Clears Up Yesterday Afternoon; Afternoon Games Commence 80

Dentsu, Tokyo, 28th: Today is the fifth day of the Far Eastern Games. The rain stopped at noon yesterday, but the wind is still strong and the temperature is low, like early autumn. The water sports competition, which is the focus of the games, will be held at the newly built outer garden swimming pool at 1:00 PM this afternoon. Athletes from China, Japan, and the Philippines are all competing in the water to win. Therefore, spectators have been flocking to the competition venue since 9:00 AM with umbrellas, lined up at the entrance. There will also be open finals in track and field, and the scene is no less grand than yesterday's competition. Before the start of the competition, there will be group exercises performed by 1,500 elementary school students and 1,200 middle school students from Tokyo, reaching the climax of the games.

(Explanation) According to yesterday's competition results, Japan has 21 points, the Philippines has 6 points, and China has 4 points. Japan has the best chance of winning the championship.

Tokyo, This Newspaper, 28th: Our country's volleyball team fought the Philippine team for the second time today, avenging their previous defeat with a score of two to zero. We won the first game 22-20 and the second game 21-15. After the victory, everyone in our country was ecstatic.

(1) First Game: Victory After Defeat 91

When the game started at 2:50 pm, Japan's Sakamoto Hirota served as the referee. The Philippines gave the ball, and Cheng Xibing from our team made a killing shot. Both sides were evenly matched. However, our side made no progress, and the Philippine team took advantage of the situation with strong attacks from the blockers and hitters on both wings. The score was initially 7-3 in favor of the Philippines. Then the two sides fought harder, with alternating wins and losses, and the ball skills displayed were excellent. Qiu Guangxie from our team was accurate and powerful in his killing shots and Xu Heng was so in his saves, and the score increased sharply. In addition, the other side lost the ball many times and was able to turn defeat into victory, and the score became 9-7 in our favor. But because the Philippine team's center, Sang Pite Luo, was tall and strong, our defense felt difficult to save the ball until we exchanged places for the 11-10. The Philippine team again had the upper hand.

After a short break, the two teams showed their spirits and fought harder. They each won and lost alternately, and they had drawn score four times. The excellent save and the power of the kill were really rare ball skills. And the quick kill shot from Qiu Guangxie of our team was especially outstanding, like an eagle falcone. After both sides scored 20 points, the game became critical. Our team finally won the first game with a wonderful serving, and also the transformation of the kill of Qiu Guangxie and the magic of Li Lianying's triangular push ball, our side got two points and won 22-20.

(II) Second Game, Bloody Battle Resulting in Victory 92

The second game began with our team initially at a disadvantage, repeatedly losing points and allowing the Philippine side to establish a four-to-two lead. Subsequently, Chen Xibing and Xu Heng's smashes, along with Li Lianying's pushes, breached the enemy's connections, reversing the decline. Afterwards, both sides frequently missed shots, and smashes often went astray. After ten changes of ends, there was little progress. Then, the Philippine team, with Sampitro's height dominating the net, gained an advantage. Coupled with Salva's smashes, their score gradually increased. Our team also scored two points. Finally, Qiu Guangxie's fierce attacks led to an eleven-to-six lead. After switching courts, our team continued to press forward with extreme ferocity. The Philippine side desperately tried to save the ball, often resulting in going out of bounds or touching the net. Afterwards, their blocking gradually became accurate and swift, and their score increased accordingly, but they still failed to tie the game with a fifteen-to-fourteen score. After their player Mengxila touched the net, their vigor was greatly diminished. Our side, with Li Lianying's quick and agile smashes, repeatedly scored, creating an eighteen-to-fourteen lead. At this point, the Philippine side requested a timeout to reorganize their formation.

When they rallied and restarted the match, it had reached a stage of hand-to-hand combat. Both sides exhausted their strengths, fighting bravely, winning and losing alternately, indistinguishable in skill. The excellence of the players' skills drew thunderous applause from the audience. Our team's smashers were skilled, and their blockers also often lightly pushed the ball, often confusing the enemy's front row, leaving them at a loss. This was especially evident today, such as Qiu Guangxie's irresistible smashes, which earned many points. As the second game ended, our team secured another victory with a score of twenty-one to fifteen, achieving a two-to-zero complete victory. The players on both sides today were as follows:

Chinese Team 93

Blockers: Zhu Zucheng, Li Lianying, Xu Heng

Smashers: Qiu Guangxie, Cao Tingzan, Chen Xibing

Retrievers: Li Fujia, Zeng Jingquan, Chen Congchao

Philippine Team 94

Blockers: Mengxila, Sampitro, Pylai

If Lin and Qiu had won, the outcome of the fifth set would have been extremely difficult to predict.

Chinese Women's Athletes Singing "Old Fisherman" at a Reception Hosted by the Japanese Women's Christian Association 115

Detailed Account of the 9th Far Eastern Games (I)

Solemn and Brilliant Opening Ceremony 116

New Greenery of the Meiji Jingu Outer Garden

Athletes from Four Countries Gather in Unity

(Tokyo Communication) The 9th Far Eastern Games, a competition for dominance in water and land sports among East Asian nations and an opportunity to connect emotionally, opened on the 24th at the Meiji Jingu Outer Garden in Tokyo. On this day, the sky was clear, the wind was gentle, and the sun was warm. At noon, 1800 participating athletes and 450 staff members entered the stadium to applause, led by the military band of the Toyama School of the Army. The first team of athletes was the Republic of China, all in white uniforms with the national emblem on their chests. They were full of spirit and high spirits, and everyone who saw them paid attention. Next was the Philippines, followed by India, and finally Japan. They circled the stadium once. At this time, the entire stadium was quiet as if no one was there. After the national anthem was played, the Vice President, Japanese Minister of Education Tanaka, read the Imperial Edict of President Prince Chichibu. Next was the opening address by President Kishii Kiyoshi, the welcoming address by Prime Minister Hamaguchi, and the congratulatory address by Kano Jigoro, a member of the International Olympic Committee. My country's Chargé d'Affaires in Japan, Jiang Hongjie, read a congratulatory telegram from Minister Wang Zhengting. This was followed by the response from the representatives of each country. First was my country's representative, Dr. Zhang Boling, followed by the Philippines, and finally India. All hoped that this conference would develop and progress, and that they would help each other in this spirit. Finally, the athletes took an oath. My country's representative, Zhang Lingjia, held the national flag by athlete Li Guochen, and the sports association flag was held by athlete Lu Ming, and two female athletes led the way to the stage to swear in Mandarin, with clear pronunciation and loud voice that resonated in the clouds. Afterwards, the representatives of the Philippines, India, and Japan also took oaths in the same manner. The Secretary-General of the Games, Hirao Ryosan, then announced the start of the competition. First, the Games flag was raised, and at the same time, thousands of male and female secondary school students sang the Games song, and thousands of pigeons were released, and two aircraft from the Asahi Shimbun and Nichinichi Shimbun flew in the sky. It was truly a grand sight. In this grand scene, the staff and athletes left the stadium, and the solemn and brilliant opening ceremony came to an end.

First Basketball Game Between China and Japan 117

Japan Defeats China 39 to 24

The Referee is Unfair, Heavily Penalizing Our Country

Tokyo Communication: At 7:30 PM on the 24th, the Chinese and Japanese basketball teams began their contact. In terms of technique, the Chinese side seemed to be slightly higher than Japan, so they thought they would have the power to win, but they were inevitably a little careless. Initially, they did not expect to lose 39 to 24. The Chinese team's poor performance greatly affected the basketball championship. It is a pity. However, the unfairness of the referee on that day was obvious to all. In the first three minutes of the game, the Chinese team was penalized seven times, which was unprecedented in basketball history. The spirit of our team members was greatly frustrated, but they were still able to endure it to the end and did not commit any irregular behavior. The spirit of sportsmanship was demonstrated. Whether one wins or loses is not worth discussing. The bias of the Japanese referee revealed their own weakness. The details of the competition are described below.

The Grand Occasion of the Stadium: The crowding of the stadium that night was unprecedented, with at least 15,000 people present. Those without tickets could not enter and stood outside the door listening for news. There were also nearly several thousand news reporters in the press box, which was even more crowded. More than a dozen photographers were constantly taking photos with magnesium lights, and the loud noise frequently hit the eardrums. The tension in the air could be said to have reached its peak.

Enthusiastic Cheerleading Squad: The cheerleading squad organized by Chinese students studying abroad and overseas Chinese all came to the venue that night, scattered in all directions, numbering no less than a thousand people. Every move of our team was greeted with thunderous cheers, and their patriotic enthusiasm was worthy of admiration. The cheerleading squad all held small national flags, and some wore red hats and white uniforms. "China, China, Long Live China" was the common slogan. At the leader's call, responses arose from all sides, which was extremely lively.

Five Goals in a Row: At the beginning of the battle, our side's momentum was strong, and the connection between Yao Enhan and Tang Baokun was extremely lively, making it difficult for the Japanese side to run and cope. However, the referee issued a penalty order within the first three minutes, penalizing us five times, and three of them were successful. They took the lead with 3 to 0. At that time, the audience was very dissatisfied and there was some commotion. Fortunately, our team members were calm and warned the crowd not to make noise and to watch the situation.

Yao and Tang Display Their Power: At this time, the little general Tang Baokun and the tumbling Yao Enhan displayed their great power, each scoring two goals, and won with 8 to 3. The military situation was greatly boosted. Unexpectedly, the order to take free throws came again, which made the brave generals dare not fight desperately, and the whole army retreated. This was the first reason for the defeat that night. In the first half, our team lost 12 to 15.

The Situation is Gone: After the lemon time, our team still used the original formation to fight. Japan, on the other hand, used Tanaka as the center and Ueda as the forward, and the military situation became more prosperous. In the second minute, Ueda continuously attacked from outside the center line and scored two goals. The record gap became wider. The center Liu Jianchang's jump balls were all seized by the Japanese. The little general Tang Shenkun's basket throwing also lost his usual accuracy. The internal gaps of Li Guochen and Wang Xiliang were also constantly exploited by the enemy. As a result, the morale of the army was disintegrating, and the situation was gone.

Change of Formation: After that, the Japanese team's score continued to increase, and the record between the two sides became further and further apart. Our team's coach, Dong Shouyi, hurriedly changed the formation, using Wang Yuzeng as the center, Wei Pengyun and Chen Shengkui as the forwards, and replacing Wang Xiliang with Lu Zhongen as the inside line. However, it was also of no avail. In the second half, our team lost 12 to 24 again. The total result was 39 to 24, and the Japanese team won.

First Day of Athletics Competition 119

No One from China Participated in the 100-Meter Preliminary

(Tokyo Communication) The 9th Far Eastern Games officially opened on May 24th. On the first day of the athletics competition, Japan won all the events except for the high jump, defeating the athletes of the three countries, and their spirit was unmatched. The results of three years of hard training are now displayed. My country relies on a few students temporarily practicing for a few times, hoping to win by luck, which is absolutely impossible. In the athletics competition, there is a scoring board with the flag of the winning country hanging. Only the Japanese flag is flying, and our country's flag has not moved at all, suffering the ridicule and contempt of the Japanese. As a reporter, I feel unspeakable pain and deeply hope that the people of our country will realize this thoroughly, work hard and practice continuously, and meet again in four years. The details of the athletics competition on the first day are described in detail below, which may also serve as a wake-up call for us.

(I) Discus Throw Final 120

The participants from our country are Lu Ming, Zhao Wenzao, and Zhang Lingjia. A solitary line is drawn for those above 30 meters, and a 30-meter sign is erected. Another solitary line is drawn for those above 35 meters, and another solitary line is drawn for those above 40 meters. The national flags of each country are inserted at the point where the athletes of each country throw. At that time, only the Japanese national flag was seen advancing one after another, and they were all above 35 meters. My country competed with the Philippines, and they were all around 30 meters. Finally, six people were selected: Japan's Saito Makoto, Kuroda Tamotsu, Okita Yoshio, and Kuniuchi Takeshi, and the Philippines' Bireya and Aiskreiter. The results were as follows:

(4) Japan's Kuniuchi Takeshi 38.39 meters

(5) Aiskreiter 33.46 meters

(6) Japan's Bireya 33.18 meters

After three more final decisions, Japan's Saito won first place with 40.27 meters, Kuroda Tamotsu was second with 39.68 meters, Okita was third with 39.01 meters, and Kuniuchi was fourth with 38.39 meters. The Far Eastern record was 38.70 meters, held by Okita Yoshi. The top three broke the Far Eastern record this time, which is truly commendable.

The participant from our country in the 1500-meter final was Jiang Yunlong. In the first lap, the Philippines' Yakv and Gray were in first and second place, and Jiang Yunlong was third. In the third lap, the Philippines only took first place, and Jiang retired to fourth. The four members of the Japanese team had gradually chased up. By the third lap, the Filipinos had no remaining strength and were overtaken by the Japanese one after another. At that time, Jiang Yunlong had fallen to the end, about 20 meters behind. By the last lap, Japan had won the first, second, third, and fourth places. Jiang was about half a lap behind, but he was still able to finish the race, and his spirit was admirable. The Far Eastern record of 4.78 seconds was held by Japan's Senda Shomon, but this time it was broken by Tsuda by about 1.8 seconds.

The Chinese participants in the long jump were Situ Guang, Wang Jihai, Zhao Rugong, and Hao Chunde. Zhao Rugong achieved the best result and was selected into the final six, who were:

(1) Japan's Nambu Chuhei: 7.59 meters
